/**
* As the manifests are loaded async, they push back page load.
* All other scripts cannot load until they have - though there is a small
* failure case if the network is terrible
*/
window.linkToScript = function (link) {

window.document.head.appendChild(script);
}
}).catch(function () { return console.warn('manifest loaded failed', link.href); });
};

if (isModernBrowser()) {

resolve(true);
};
}
else {
resolve(false);
}
});

fepPrimaryProduct: fep.primaryProduct,
fepSecondaryProducts: fep.secondaryProducts,
fepCompanies: fep.companies,
fepCategory: fep.category,
fepGroups: fep.groups,
fepPrimaryCompany: fep.primaryCompany,
primaryCategory: fep.primaryCategory,
secondaryCategories: fep.secondaryCategories,
tertiaryCategories: fep.tertiaryCategories,
}));
}
window.bordeaux.setPageTemplate("home");
window.bordeaux.init();
});
  </script>

       <div class="listing__text-wrapper">
        <h2 class="listing__title">
         Google Pixel 6 set to drop signature fingerprint scanner for under display reader
        </h2>
        <p class="listing__text listing__text--strapline">
